add_namespace = ireland
add_namespace = irelandflavour

 ### CONTENTS ###
 # Intro								(ireland.0 -> ireland.6)
 # Black Monday / Ulster Comes First	(ireland.7 -> ireland.12)
 # Pre-Elections						(ireland.13 -> ireland.20)
 # Elections / Black Monday outcome		(ireland.21 -> ireland.47)
 # Influence Mechanic / Civil Rights	(ireland.1000 -> ireland.1499)
 # Focuses								(ireland.1500 -> ireland.1999)
 # Forpol								(ireland.2000 -> ireland.2499)
 # Democratic Events					(ireland.2500 -> ireland.2999)
 # Reactionary Events					(ireland.3000 -> ireland.3499)
 # Socialist Events						(ireland.3500 -> ireland.3999)
 # News Events							(ireland.4000 -> ireland.4499)
 # 1941 Election Tree Events			(ireland.4500 -> ireland.4999)
 # MIOs									(ireland.5000 -> ireland.5499)
 # AI Pathing							(ireland.5500 -> ireland.5999)
 # Hidden Events						(ireland.6000 -> ireland.6499)
 # Resistance Events					(ireland.6500 -> ireland.6599)
 # Flavour Events						(irelandflavour)

 # Intro #

country_event = {  # The State of the Republic, 1936
	id = ireland.0
	title = ireland.0.t
	desc = ireland.0.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_great_seal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.0 option ireland.0.a"
		name = ireland.0.a
	}
}

country_event = {  # Model Republic
	id = ireland.1
	title = ireland.1.t
	desc = ireland.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_street
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1 option ireland.1.a"
		name = ireland.1.a
		add_political_power = 20
	}
}

country_event = {  # George is dead
	id = ireland.2
	title = ireland.2.t
	desc = ireland.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_death_george
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2 option ireland.2.a"
		name = ireland.2.a  # Not our concern
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		add_political_power = 10
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2 option ireland.2.b"
		name = ireland.2.b  # Send a private telegram
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		add_political_power = -5
		CAN = { country_event = { id = ireland.3 days = 2 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2 option ireland.2.c"
		name = ireland.2.c  # Give a speech
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		add_political_power = -20
		country_event = { id = ireland.5 days = 2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gave_speech days = 30 value = 1 }
				country_event = { id = ireland.3 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Canada gets telegram / hears of speech
	id = ireland.3
	title = ireland.3.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_gave_speech } }
		text = ireland.3.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_gave_speech }
		text = ireland.3.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.3 option ireland.3.a"
		name = ireland.3.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_gave_speech } }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = ireland.4 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.3 option ireland.3.b"
		name = ireland.3.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_gave_speech }
	}
}

 # Black Monday / Ulster Comes First #

country_event = {  # Black Monday (07/02/36, originally triggered by black.1, fires 3 days after BM)
	id = ireland.7
	title = ireland.7.t
	desc = ireland.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_crowd
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {	# Note - please do not remove the immediates / effect tooltips in this event chain, as it can unbalance the minigame if players hold events
		hidden_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_political_power = -30
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_german_eco_dominance_base
				add_idea = IRE_black_monday_1
			}
			country_event = { id = ireland.8 days = 5 } #  UDP is pissed
			country_event = { id = ireland.9 days = 19 } #  The Empty Factories
			country_event = { id = ireland.10 days = 33 } #  The Silent Ports
		#	country_event = { id = ireland.13 days = 47 } #  Stitchies & Pinnies - triggered by history
			country_event = { id = ireland.11 days = 61 } #  Life Among Ghosts
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.7 option ireland.7.a"
		name = ireland.7.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_political_power = -30
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_german_eco_dominance_base
				add_idea = IRE_black_monday_1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  #  UDP is pissed. 12/02/36
	id = ireland.8
	title = ireland.8.t
	desc = ireland.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_brooke_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {  # this is to reset pp if the player has held focuses etc
			if = {
				limit = { has_political_power > 43 }
				set_political_power = 43
			}
			activate_mission = IRE_UCF_mission
			add_stability = -0.1
			set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.35 }
			IRE_loyalist_anger_increase = yes
			set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ongoing
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.8 option ireland.8.a"
		name = ireland.8.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.8.a.tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			unlock_national_focus = IRE_assess_bm
			activate_mission = IRE_UCF_mission
			add_stability = -0.1
			set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.35 }
			IRE_loyalist_anger_increase = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Black Monday 1 - The Empty Factories
	id = ireland.9
	title = ireland.9.t
	desc = ireland.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_alufactory
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -3 }
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -35
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.9 option ireland.9.a"
		name = ireland.9.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.9.a.tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -35
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # End of UCF. 12th of August.
	id = ireland.12
	title = ireland.12.t

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco > 5 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 5 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ww }
		}
		text = ireland.12.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco > 5 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 0 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_wl }
		}
		text = ireland.12.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 5 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_lw }
		}
		text = ireland.12.d3

	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 0 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ll }
		}
		text = ireland.12.d4
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 1 }
		}
		text = ireland.12.d5
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = IRE_emergency_taxes_idea
			remove_ideas = IRE_austerity_idea
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.12 option ireland.12.a"
		name = ireland.12.a
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco > 5 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 5 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ww }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = 0.10
		add_political_power = 75
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.35 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_nationalist_discontent_delta = 0.03 }
		IRE_nationalist_discontent_increase = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fullsuccess
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.12 option ireland.12.b"
		name = ireland.12.b
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco > 5 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 0 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_wl }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 75
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.3 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ecosuccess
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.12 option ireland.12.c"
		name = ireland.12.c
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 5 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_lw }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 50
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.35 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_nationalist_discontent_delta = 0.03 }
		IRE_nationalist_discontent_increase = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_northsuccess
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.12 option ireland.12.e"
		name = ireland.12.e
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_eco < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 6 }
				check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north > 0 }
			}
			else = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ll }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.025
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.3 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fail
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.12 option ireland.12.f"
		name = ireland.12.f
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { IRE_UCF_north < 1 }
		}
		IRE_initial_eco_measures = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCF_gigafail
	}
}

}

country_event = {  # SocDem and SocLib urban/rural
	id = ireland.20
	title = ireland.20.t
	desc = ireland.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_obrien
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			if = {	# for some reason the AI doesn't generate the same amount of pp up to that day as a player can
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ww
						has_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_lw
					}
					has_political_power < 52
				}
				set_political_power = 52
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.20 option ireland.20.a"
		name = ireland.20.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.01
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ireland.23

	desc = ireland.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_mulcahy
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fullsuccess } }

	option = {	# Mulcahy takeover
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.23 option ireland.23.a"
		name = ireland.23.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_sf_collins } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ecosuccess
					has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_northsuccess
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fail
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_collins_stands_aside_tt
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ireland.24 days = 5 } }
	}
	option = {	# Collins stays put
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.23 option ireland.23.b"
		name = ireland.23.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_sf_mulcahy } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ecosuccess
					has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_northsuccess
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -25
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fail
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_collins_stays_put_tt
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ireland.25 days = 5 } }
	}
}

country_event = {  # 1937 Election event
	id = ireland.31
	title = ireland.31.t
	desc = ireland.31.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_old_woman_voting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 4

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.31 option ireland.31.a"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland elects Sinn Fein with Collins"
		name = ireland.31.a	# SF Collins
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = { IRE_sf_influence > IRE_sc_influence }
					check_variable = { IRE_sf_influence > IRE_lab_influence }
					has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_collins
				}
				has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_sf_collins
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fullsuccess }
			add_political_power = 125
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 150 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_remove_elecpath = yes
			IRE_load_sf_govt_advisors = yes
			complete_national_focus = IRE_sinn_fein
			news_event = { id = ireland.4000 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.43 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.1003 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.31 option ireland.31.b"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland elects Sinn Fein with Mulcahy"
		name = ireland.31.b	# SF Mulcahy
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = { IRE_sf_influence > IRE_sc_influence }
					check_variable = { IRE_sf_influence > IRE_lab_influence }
					has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_mulcahy
				}
				has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_sf_mulcahy
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 150
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		add_country_leader_trait = IRE_the_reformer
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_remove_elecpath = yes
			IRE_load_sf_govt_advisors = yes
			complete_national_focus = IRE_sinn_fein
			set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gen_mulcahy days = 20 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.42 days = 5 }
			news_event = { id = ireland.4025 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.43 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.1003 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.31 option ireland.31.c"
		name = ireland.31.c	# SC
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = { IRE_sc_influence > IRE_sf_influence }
					check_variable = { IRE_sc_influence > IRE_lab_influence }
				}
				IRE_sc_election = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		IRE_remove_govt_flag = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_govt_sc_temp
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		country_event = { id = ireland.32 days = 5 }
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE_remove_elecpath = yes
			IRE_load_temp_advisors = yes
			activate_advisor = IRE_dail_eireann_sic
			complete_national_focus = IRE_saorstat_criostuil
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.31 option ireland.31.e"
		name = ireland.31.e	# Labour
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = no
					check_variable = { IRE_lab_influence > IRE_sf_influence }
					check_variable = { IRE_lab_influence > IRE_sc_influence }
				}
				IRE_lab_election = yes
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}

country_event = {  # Negotiations with the NDP (Dev)
	id = ireland.33
	title = ireland.33.t

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fullsuccess
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_ecosuccess
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_northsuccess
			}
		}
		text = ireland.33.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fail
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_gigafail
			}
		}
		text = ireland.33.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_lemass
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 4

	option = {	# NDP Coalition
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.33 option ireland.33.a"
		name = ireland.33.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = DEFAULT }
				has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_CENTRIST_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_parliamentary_an
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_abstentionist_an
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_an
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.33.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_election_sc_ndp days = 30 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.34 days = 5 }
		}
	}
	option = {	# Blueshirt coup
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.33 option ireland.33.b"
		name = ireland.33.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = DEFAULT }
				has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_ndp
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_sc
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_an
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.33.b.tt
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ireland.35 days = 5 } }
	}
	option = {	# Cursed Coalition
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.33 option ireland.33.c"
		name = ireland.33.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_fail
				has_country_flag = IRE_UCF_gigafail
			}
			OR = {
				is_ai = no
				has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = DEFAULT }
				has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_CURSED_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_parliamentary_an
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_abstentionist_an
					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_ndp
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.33.c.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_election_sc_an days = 30 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.34 days = 5 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Coalition decided
	id = ireland.34
	title = ireland.34.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_election_sc_ndp }
		text = ireland.34.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_election_sc_an }
		text = ireland.34.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_dev_group
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 4

	option = {	# NDP Coalition
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.34 option ireland.34.a"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland elects SC with NDP"
		name = ireland.34.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_election_sc_ndp }
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.34.a.tt
		IRE_remove_govt_flag = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_govt_sc_ndp
		IRE_sean_lemass_add_sic_tt = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 150
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			IRE_load_sc_ndp_govt_advisors = yes
			activate_advisor = IRE_sean_lemass_sic
			set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gen_SF_to_dem days = 20 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.42 days = 5 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.43 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.1003 days = 15 }
			news_event = { id = ireland.4050 }
		}
	}
	option = {	# Cursed Coalition
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.34 option ireland.34.b"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland elects SC with AN"
		name = ireland.34.b
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_election_sc_an }
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.34.b.tt
		IRE_remove_govt_flag = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition
		IRE_eoin_oduffy_add_sic_tt = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 150
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.05 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_increase = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			IRE_load_cursed_coalition_govt_advisors = yes
			IRE_eoin_oduffy = { ### IRE TEMP - wait for scripted loc fix
				remove_second_in_command_role = yes
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = IRE_eoin_oduffy
					advisor = {
						slot = second_in_command
						idea_token = IRE_eoin_oduffy_cursed_sic
						traits = { KR_old_general_sic }
						cost = 0
						can_be_fired = no
					}
					activate = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gen_SF_to_dem days = 20 value = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.42 days = 5 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.43 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.1003 days = 15 }
			news_event = { id = ireland.4075 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = IRE_black_monday_1
						has_idea = IRE_black_monday_2
						has_idea = IRE_black_monday_3
						has_idea = IRE_black_monday_4
						has_idea = IRE_black_monday_5
						has_idea = IRE_black_monday_6
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = IRE_AN_extra_bm_focuses
				if = {
					limit = { is_ai = no }
					set_country_flag = IRE_SCAN_can_repeat_focus
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = ireland.45.t
	desc = ireland.45.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_bm_failed days = 100 value = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.45 option ireland.45.a"
		name = ireland.45.a
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.05
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -0.05 }
			IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		}
		IRE_fail_bm = yes
		clr_country_flag = IRE_collins_success
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = 50
				add_stability = 0.10
				set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.05 }
				IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
				IRE_finish_bm_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # LÉ Macha Incident
	id = ireland.1000

	title = {
		trigger = { tag = IRE }
		text = ireland.1000.t.IRE
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = IRE } }
		text = ireland.1000.t.other
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = { tag = IRE }
		text = ireland.1000.d.IRE
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { is_second_in_command = yes }
		}
		text = ireland.1000.d.GER.autdem
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			GER_hermann_muller = { is_second_in_command = yes }
		}
		text = ireland.1000.d.GER.socdem
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			GER_ewald_von_kleist_schmenzin = { is_second_in_command = yes }
		}
		text = ireland.1000.d.GER.pataut
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { tag = ENG }
		text = ireland.1000.d.ENG
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_le_macha
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { tag = IRE }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = { IRE_favour_cost = 10 }
				set_variable = { IRE_gateway_GER_pressure_duration = 10 }
				set_variable = { IRE_gateway_ENG_pressure_duration = 10 }
				set_country_flag = IRE_gateway_started
				GER = { country_event = ireland.1000 }
				ENG = { country_event = ireland.1000 }
				IRE_remove_UCFpath = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = IRE decision = GER_pressure_ireland }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = IRE decision = GER_pressure_ireland_guns }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = IRE decision = GER_pressure_ireland_cp }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = IRE decision = GER_pressure_ireland_xp }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = ENG }
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = IRE decision = ENG_pressure_ireland }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = IRE decision = ENG_pressure_ireland_guns }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = IRE decision = ENG_pressure_ireland_cp }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = IRE decision = ENG_pressure_ireland_xp }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1000 option ireland.1000.a.IRE"
		name = ireland.1000.a.IRE
		trigger = { tag = IRE }
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_gateway_IRE_start_tt
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			complete_national_focus = IRE_le_macha_incident
			country_event = { id = ireland.1001 days = 5 }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = IRE_favour_a_side_GER }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENG decision = IRE_favour_a_side_ENG }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1000 option ireland.1000.a.GER"
		name = ireland.1000.a.GER
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_gateway_start_tt
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1000 option ireland.1000.a.ENG"
		name = ireland.1000.a.ENG
		trigger = { tag = ENG }
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_gateway_start_tt
	}
}

					activate_mission = IRE_GER_gateway_short_countdown
				}
				ENG = {
					country_event = ireland.1022
					remove_mission = IRE_ENG_gateway_long_countdown
					activate_mission = IRE_ENG_gateway_short_countdown
				}
				119 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IRE_gateway_short_countdown_idea
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1022 option ireland.1022.a"
		name = ireland.1022.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = IRE }
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = IRE_gateway_short_countdown }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			119 = {
				damage_building = { type = infrastructure damage = 1 }
				damage_building = { type = industrial_complex damage = 1 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = IRE_GER_gateway_short_countdown }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.1022.tt
	}

				remove_mission = IRE_gateway_long_countdown
				activate_mission = IRE_gateway_short_countdown
				GER = {
					country_event = ireland.1023
					remove_mission = IRE_GER_gateway_long_countdown
					activate_mission = IRE_GER_gateway_short_countdown
				}
				ENG = {
					country_event = ireland.1023
					remove_mission = IRE_ENG_gateway_long_countdown
					activate_mission = IRE_ENG_gateway_short_countdown
				}
				119 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IRE_gateway_short_countdown_idea
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1023 option ireland.1023.a"
		name = ireland.1023.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = IRE }
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = IRE_gateway_short_countdown }
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = { activate_mission = IRE_GER_gateway_short_countdown }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.1022.tt
	}

		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = 0.1

			limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party < 0.50 } }
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.10 }
			IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.05 }
			IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_collins_success }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			swap_ruler_traits = { remove = IRE_big_fellow_1 add = IRE_big_fellow_2 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.1051.a.tt2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { IRE_has_reactionary_govt = no }
				country_event = { id = ireland.1053 days = 365 }			### Constitution
				ENT = { country_event = { id = canada.150 days = 5 } }		### Human CAN invite IRE?
			}
			else = {
				IRE_determine_NIR_revolt = yes
				IRE_remove_extremepolpath = yes
			}
			IRE_remove_gateway_decisions = yes
		}
	}
}

						ideology = social_liberal
						popularity = 0.10
					}
					add_ideas = IRE_tenuous_coalition
					add_ideas = IRE_GER_puppet_idea
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			IRE_sean_lemass_add_sic_tt = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.10
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.10
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			add_ideas = IRE_tenuous_coalition
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			add_ideas = IRE_GER_puppet_idea
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line

				GER = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ROOT

						end_wars = no
					}
				}
			}

				GER = { country_event = ireland.1125 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				get_current_government_type = yes
				GER = {
					add_to_faction = IRE
					set_autonomy = {
						target = IRE
						autonomy_state = autonomous_puppet
						end_wars = no
					}
				}
				restore_previous_government_type = yes
				complete_national_focus = IRE_labour
				IRE_william_obrien = {
					remove_country_leader_role_social_democrat = yes

							desc = IRE_william_obrien_ger_aligned_leader_desc

							traits = { IRE_dedicated_unioniser }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				IRE_sean_lemass = {
					remove_country_leader_role_market_liberal = yes

					}

		trigger = {
			IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = yes
			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_IRE_victory
		}
		text = ireland.1200.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = yes
			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_GER_victory
		}
		text = ireland.1200.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = IRE_northern_catholics }
		}
		text = ireland.1200.d3
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes
			has_completed_focus = IRE_northern_catholics
		}
		text = ireland.1200.d4
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes }
		text = ireland.1200.d5
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_orange_order_2
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1200 option ireland.1200.a"
		name = ireland.1200.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = yes
				AND = {
					IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes
					has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_GER_victory
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1200 option ireland.1200.b"
		name = ireland.1200.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes
					has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_IRE_victory
				}
				IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_northern_catholics }
				set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.05 }
				IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
				119 = { add_compliance = 7.5 }
				set_variable = { IRE_ulster_resistance_delta = 0.075 }
				add_to_variable = { IRE_ulster_resistance = IRE_ulster_resistance_delta }
				force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_reluctant_countrymen_modified
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_ulster_resistance_target_change_tt
				IRE_update_resistance = yes
			}
			else = { activate_mission = IRE_counter_protestant_influence }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.05 }
			IRE_loyalist_anger_increase = yes
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes
				has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_IRE_victory
			}
			IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1201 option ireland.1201.a"
		name = ireland.1201.a
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes }
			set_variable = { IRE_NIR_decisions_time = 15 }
			set_variable = { IRE_NIR_mission_time = 30 }
			set_variable = { IRE_NIR_mission_time_long = 45 }
			set_variable = { IRE_NIR_decisions_time_long = 25 }
			add_to_variable = { IRE_NIR_decisions_variable = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_timed_halved_effect
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_AN_NIR_revolt_available_tt
			set_country_flag = IRE_NIR_revolt_available
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes }
			set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.05 }
			IRE_loyalist_anger_increase = yes
		}
	}
}

	}
	option = {

		name = ireland.1202.b

			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -0.025 }
			IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.1202 option ireland.1202.c"
		name = ireland.1202.c

			has_global_flag = IRE_had_NIR_revolt

			remove_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = IRE_join_reichspakt }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = ENT decision = IRE_join_entente }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = INT decision = IRE_join_internationale }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = RUS decision = IRE_join_moscow_accord }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = JAP decision = IRE_join_copro }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
				remove_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = IRE_seek_guarantee_germany }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2001 option ireland.2001.a.GER1"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland joins Reichspakt"
		name = ireland.2001.a.GER1
		trigger = {
			FROM = { tag = GER }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_desperate_measures }
		}
		FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		clr_country_flag = IRE_joining_faction
		set_country_flag = IRE_spindler_event
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = GER_stay_out_france_uk
				any_state = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				IMP = { exists = yes }
				ENT = { exists = yes }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
					transfer_state_to = IMP
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		}
		IRE_replace_erin_go_bragh_idea = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2001 option ireland.2001.a.GER2"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland joins Reichspakt after Entente dies"
		name = ireland.2001.a.GER2
		trigger = {
			FROM = { tag = GER }
			has_country_flag = IRE_desperate_measures
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				save_event_target_as = peace_country

				# first peace out with faction leaders
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
					}
					event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
				}

				# then all non-puppets whose faction leaders aren't in the war
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction = yes
						faction_leader = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
						NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
					}
					event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
				}

				# then all non-puppets who aren't in factions
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction = no
						NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
					}
					event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
				}

				# then all puppets whose overlords aren't in the war
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_subject = yes
						overlord = { NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
						NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
					}
					event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		clr_country_flag = IRE_joining_faction
		clr_country_flag = IRE_desperate_measures
		set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_desperate_measures days = 5 value = 1 }
		clr_country_flag = IRE_1916_entente_event
		set_country_flag = IRE_spindler_event
		IRE_replace_erin_go_bragh_idea = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = IRE_better_the_devil
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2001 option ireland.2001.a.ENT1"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland joins Entente"
		name = ireland.2001.a.ENT1
		trigger = {
			FROM = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_desperate_measures }
		}
		ENT = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		clr_country_flag = IRE_joining_faction
		set_country_flag = IRE_1916_entente_event

		hidden_effect = {

		}

	}

					}

				}

						NOT = { has_war_with = ENT }
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = INT }
					}
					event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
				}

				# then all non-puppets who aren't in factions

	id = ireland.2004
	title = ireland.2004.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
		text = ireland.2004.d.GER
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { FROM = { is_american_tag = yes } }
		text = ireland.2004.d.USA
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
			GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2004 option ireland.2004.a.GER"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Germany guarantees Ireland"
		name = ireland.2004.a.GER
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
		if = {
			limit = { GER_is_in_mitteleuropa = yes }
			FROM = { give_guarantee = ROOT }
			set_country_flag = IRE_got_guarantee_@FROM
		}
		clr_country_flag = IRE_seeking_guarantee
		clr_country_flag = IRE_joining_faction
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = IRE_seek_guarantee_germany }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2004 option ireland.2004.a.USA"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;America guarantees Ireland"
		name = ireland.2004.a.USA
		trigger = { FROM = { is_american_tag = yes } }
		FROM = { give_guarantee = ROOT }
		set_country_flag = IRE_got_guarantee_@FROM
		clr_country_flag = IRE_seeking_guarantee
		clr_country_flag = IRE_joining_faction
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = ACC }
				JAP = {
					has_democratic_government = yes
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_country_flag = ACW_supported_ACC
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = HAW
						has_war_with = ROOT
						has_war_with = ACC
					}
				}
				ACC = {
					OR = {
						is_in_faction = no
						is_in_faction_with = JAP
					}
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = USA_fortress_america }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = USA_rebuild_monroe }
				}
			}
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = JAP decision = IRE_join_copro }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = USA decision = IRE_seek_guarantee_america }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = WCA decision = IRE_seek_guarantee_america }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = APG decision = IRE_seek_guarantee_america }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = ACC decision = IRE_seek_guarantee_america }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = NEE decision = IRE_seek_guarantee_america }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Join MA?
	id = ireland.2008
	title = ireland.2008.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_democratic_government = yes }
		text = ireland.2008.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_democratic_government = no }
		text = ireland.2008.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes 		### on_action

	trigger = {
		GER = { exists = no }
		has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_IRE_victory
		is_in_faction = no
		NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
		OR = {
			has_war = no
			all_enemy_country = { has_war_with = RUS }
		}
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		INT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
		OR = {
			AND = {
				RUS = { has_elected_government = yes }
				ROOT = { has_democratic_government = yes }
			}
			AND = {
				RUS = { has_authoritarian_government = yes }
				ROOT = { has_dictatorship_government = yes }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_democratic_government = yes }
			OR = {
				FRA = { has_government = totalist }
				ENG = { has_government = totalist }
				64 = { owner = { is_in_faction_with = INT } }
				AND = {
					INT = { has_war_with = FROM }
					INT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_rejected_guarantee_USA
					NOT = { country_exists = USA }
					USA = { same_government_type_as_ROOT = no }
					USA = { is_subject = yes }
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_rejected_guarantee_APG
					NOT = { country_exists = APG }
					APG = { same_government_type_as_ROOT = no }
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_rejected_guarantee_ACC
					NOT = { country_exists = ACC }
					ACC = { same_government_type_as_ROOT = no }
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_rejected_guarantee_NEE
					NOT = { country_exists = NEE }
					NEE = { same_government_type_as_ROOT = no }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
					CAN = { has_war_with = WCA }
					country_exists = USA
					country_exists = APG
					country_exists = ACC
					country_exists = NEE
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2008 option ireland.2008.a"
		name = ireland.2008.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				UKR = { has_country_flag = UKR_small_pact_tree }
			}
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = RUS decision = IRE_join_moscow_accord }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2008 option ireland.2008.b"
		name = ireland.2008.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				UKR = { has_country_flag = UKR_small_pact_tree }
			}
		}
	}
}

						}
					}
				}
			}

		else = {

			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = IRE_SCW_volunteers

					limit = { is_ai = no }

						set_country_flag = IRE_supported_SPA
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { FROM = { tag = SPR } }
						set_country_flag = IRE_supported_SPR
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { FROM = { tag = SWF } }
						set_country_flag = IRE_supported_SWF
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {  # Reaction to joining Entente
	id = ireland.2017
	title = ireland.2017.t
	desc = ireland.2017.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_entente
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2017 option ireland.2017.a"
		name = ireland.2017.a
		add_stability = -0.025
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_loyalist_anger_delta = 0.025 }
		IRE_loyalist_anger_decrease = yes
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = IMP }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					is_ireland = no
					OR = {
						is_great_britain = yes
						is_claimed_by = IMP
						is_core_of = IMP
					}
				}
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					is_ireland = no
					OR = {
						is_great_britain = yes
						is_claimed_by = IMP
						is_core_of = IMP
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = IMP
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_targeted_decision = { target = var:133.owner decision = IRE_reclaim_gaelic_lands }
				clear_variable = IRE_war_decision_days
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = IRE_monarchist_gael }
					set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_monarchist
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = IRE_regency_gael }
					set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_regency
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_country_flag = IRE_polpath_41_cnat

country_event = {  # The Opposition Coalesces
	id = ireland.2505
	title = ireland.2505.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_autdem_govt = yes }
		text = ireland.2505.d.sf
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_soccon_in_coalition = yes }
		text = ireland.2505.d.sc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_socdem_in_coalition = yes }
		text = ireland.2505.d.labour
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2505 option ireland.2505.a"
		name = ireland.2505.a
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_socdem_in_coalition = no }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@social_democrat < 0.10 } }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.075
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_soccon_in_coalition = no }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@social_conservative < 0.10 } }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.075
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_autdem_govt = no }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_sf_marlib }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat < 0.10 } }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 0.075
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 0.05
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { party_popularity@market_liberal < 0.10 } }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = market_liberal
						popularity = 0.075
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = market_liberal
						popularity = 0.05
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.025
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.025
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = -0.025
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.025
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	# Post-War SF turn MarLib?
	id = ireland.2550			### can be triggered by on_actions
	title = ireland.2550.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_collins }
		text = ireland.2550.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_mulcahy }
		text = ireland.2550.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
		text = ireland.2550.d3
	}

	picture = "[IRE_loc_victory_event_pic]"
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = IRE
		IRE_has_autdem_govt = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_sf_marlib }
		FRA = { exists = no }
		OR = {
			ENG = {
				OR = {
					exists = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = IRE_treaty_london
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_IRE_victory
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_GER_victory
				GER = { has_elected_government = yes }
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				focus_progress = { focus = IRE_draft_new_constitution progress > 0 }
			}
			has_completed_focus = IRE_draft_new_constitution
		}
		has_country_flag = IRE_had_war_with_INT
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_brooke_advisor_postwar
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENT }
				}
				NIR_basil_brooke = {
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = political_advisor
							idea_token = NIR_basil_brooke_advisor
							traits = { KR_consummate_proceduralist }
							cost = 150
							can_be_fired = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = IRE_had_war_with_INT
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2550 option ireland.2550.a"
		name = ireland.2550.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
			custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.2550.a.tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep_delayed_elections }
				clr_country_flag = IRE_parlrep_delayed_elections
				country_event = { id = ireland.2511 days = 5 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_will_have_parlrep }
				country_event = { id = ireland.2510 days = 5 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_brooke_advisor_postwar
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENT }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.2560.a.tt3
				show_ideas_tooltip = NIR_basil_brooke_advisor
				custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.2601.a.tt2
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_advisor = NIR_basil_brooke_advisor
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				IRE_disband_wartime_coalition = yes
				clr_country_flag = IRE_brooke_advisor_postwar
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep }
					var:IRE.IRE_former_president = { promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
					IRE_michael_collins = { remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes }
					activate_advisor = IRE_michael_collins_sic
					clear_variable = IRE_former_president
				}
				else = { activate_advisor = IRE_dail_eireann_sic }
			}
		}
		IRE_sf_turn_marlib = yes
		add_political_power = 20
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_had_megacollins
				NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep }
			}
			country_event = { id = ireland.2503 days = 5 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { unlock_national_focus = IRE_repeal_civil_restrictions }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2550 option ireland.2550.b"
		name = ireland.2550.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_sf_megacollins }
			custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.2550.a.tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep_delayed_elections }
				clr_country_flag = IRE_parlrep_delayed_elections
				country_event = { id = ireland.2511 days = 5 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep }
				IRE_michael_collins_parlrep_sic_tt = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_will_have_parlrep }
				country_event = { id = ireland.2510 days = 5 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			}
			else = {
				IRE_richard_mulcahy_add_sic_tt = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_brooke_advisor_postwar
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENT }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.2560.a.tt3
				show_ideas_tooltip = NIR_basil_brooke_advisor
				custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.2601.a.tt2
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_advisor = NIR_basil_brooke_advisor
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				IRE_disband_wartime_coalition = yes
				clr_country_flag = IRE_brooke_advisor_postwar
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep }
					var:IRE.IRE_former_president = { promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
					IRE_michael_collins = { remove_all_country_leader_roles = yes }
					activate_advisor = IRE_michael_collins_sic
					clear_variable = IRE_former_president
				}
				else = {
					deactivate_advisor = IRE_richard_mulcahy_army_chief
					activate_advisor = IRE_richard_mulcahy_sic
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = { unlock_national_focus = IRE_repeal_civil_restrictions }
	}
}

					}

				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = DEFAULT } }

		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line

		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.2560.a.tt4

				}
			}

country_event = {  # End of Constitution Chain
	id = ireland.2607
	title = ireland.2607.t
	desc = ireland.2607.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_dail_chamber
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 10

	immediate = {
		add_to_variable = { IRE_new_constitution_stab = -0.05 }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2607 option ireland.2607.a"
		name = ireland.2607.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_new_constitution_end_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_new_constitution_modifier_tt
		add_to_variable = { IRE_new_constitution_stab = 0.05 }
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = IRE_new_constitution_temp
				add_idea = IRE_new_constitution
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_will_have_parlrep }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_parlrep_postwar } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				country_event = { id = ireland.2510 days = 5 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_parlrep_postwar_tt
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_federalisation_wip }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = EFFECT_UNLOCK_DECISION_CATEGORY
				NAME = IRE_federalisation
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_federalisation_outcome_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = 113 decision = IRE_federal_assembly }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = 119 decision = IRE_federal_assembly }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = 135 decision = IRE_federal_assembly }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = 134 decision = IRE_federal_assembly }
				set_variable = { IRE_improve_nationalist_discontent_cost = 25 }
				set_variable = { IRE_improve_loyalist_anger_cost = 25 }
				set_variable = { IRE_decision_duration = 15 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			complete_national_focus = IRE_draft_new_constitution
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = IRE_new_constitution_modifier
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_bop_jjok }
				country_event = { id = ireland.3100 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_GER_victory
			IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = yes
		}
		text = ireland.2608.d3
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_GER_victory
			IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes
		}
		text = ireland.2608.d4
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_ENG_victory }
		text = ireland.2608.d5
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		IRE_has_puppet_govt = no
		owns_state = 119 # Northern Ireland
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.2608 option ireland.2608.a"
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;Ireland removes Ulster Privileges"
		name = ireland.2608.a
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = 0.05
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.025 }
		IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_ni_secure
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_nir_resistance_started
				IRE_has_reactionary_govt = yes
			}
			clr_country_flag = IRE_nir_resistance_started
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = IRE_had_NIR_revolt }
				119 = {
					add_compliance = 15
					enable_state_integration_80_compliance = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_reluctant_countrymen_modified
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_an_ulster_remove_revolt_tt
				add_to_variable = { IRE.IRE_ulster_local_resource_factor = 0.15 }
				add_to_variable = { IRE.IRE_ulster_local_manpower = 0.05 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_reluctant_countrymen_modified
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_an_ulster_remove_no_revolt_tt
				add_to_variable = { IRE.IRE_ulster_local_resource_factor = 0.15 }
				add_to_variable = { IRE.IRE_ulster_local_manpower = 0.15 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_nir_resistance_started
				IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes
			}
			clr_country_flag = IRE_nir_resistance_started
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = IRE_had_NIR_revolt }
				119 = {
					add_compliance = 15
					enable_state_integration_80_compliance = yes
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_reluctant_countrymen_modified
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_soc_ulster_remove_revolt_tt
				add_to_variable = { IRE.IRE_ulster_local_resource_factor = 0.15 }
				add_to_variable = { IRE.IRE_ulster_local_manpower = 0.35 }
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_reluctant_countrymen_modified
				custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_soc_ulster_remove_no_revolt_tt
				add_to_variable = { IRE.IRE_ulster_local_resource_factor = 0.15 }
				add_to_variable = { IRE.IRE_ulster_local_manpower = 0.45 }
			}
		}
	}

	desc = {

	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = IRE_aodh_o_neill } }
		text = ireland.3300.d2
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = IRE
		has_government = national_populist
		is_in_faction_with = RUS
		RUS = { has_government = national_populist }
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			NFA = {
				has_government = national_populist

				has_government = national_populist

			}

				is_subject = no
			}

				is_subject = no
			}
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_leinster_house

	fire_only_once = yes

			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			complete_national_focus = IRE_the_regency
			hidden_effect = {
				IRE_aodh_o_neill = { remove_country_leader_role_national_populist = yes }
				IRE_gearoid_o_cuinneagain = { set_character_as_republican = yes }
				activate_advisor = IRE_jj_walsh_sic

					focus = IRE_the_restoration

					}

					}
				}

unit_leader_event = {  # IRE event for EDS
	id = ireland.3725
	title = ireland.3725.t
	desc = ireland.3725.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			ROOT = {
				ENG_eric_dorman_smith = {
					demote_to_general = yes
					remove_military_advisor_roles = yes
					if = {
						limit = { has_trait = panzer_expert }
						remove_unit_leader_trait = panzer_expert
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_trait = combined_arms_expert }
						remove_unit_leader_trait = combined_arms_expert
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_global_flag = IRE_gaelicisation }
						set_character_name = IRE_eric_dorman_smith_alt
					}
					else = {
						set_character_name = IRE_eric_dorman_smith
					}
					set_portraits = {
						army = {
							large = GFX_portrait_IRE_eric_dorman_smith_army_large
							small = GFX_portrait_IRE_eric_dorman_smith_army_small
						}
					}
					set_leader_description = IRE_eric_dorman_smith_high_command_desc
					add_advisor_role = {
						advisor = {
							slot = high_command
							idea_token = IRE_eric_dorman_smith_high_command
							ledger = army
							traits = { KR_MHC_armoured_2 }
							cost = 100
							ai_will_do = { factor = 0 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.3725 option ireland.3725.a"
		name = ireland.3725.a
		effect_tooltip = { ENG_eric_dorman_smith = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
	}
}

country_event = {  # Asking a country to invest
	id = ireland.4500
	title = ireland.4500.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = no }
		text = ireland.4500.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		text = ireland.4500.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_alufactory
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.4500 option ireland.4500.a"
		name = ireland.4500.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				has_opinion = { target = IRE value < -20 }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_ideas = IRE_irish_trade_partner
		IRE = {
			country_event = { id = ireland.4550 days = 2 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.4500 option ireland.4500.b"
		name = ireland.4500.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				has_opinion = { target = FROM value > 30 }
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			country_event = { id = ireland.4525 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Country said yes
	id = ireland.4550
	title = ireland.4550.t
	desc = "[FROM.IRE_investment_response_event_desc]"
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory_construction

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.4550 option ireland.4550.a"
		name = ireland.4550.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ireland.4550.a.tt		# If editing any of these, be sure to edit the loc tooltip aswell
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IRE_investment_slots
			value = 0.01
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IRE_investment_industrial
			value = 0.02
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = IRE_investment_milestone
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { IRE_investment_milestone = 4 }
			}
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { IRE_investment_milestone = 9 }
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = ireland.4500.t # Name would be weird otherwise
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = electronics
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { IRE_investment_milestone = 14 }
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = ireland.4500.t # Name would be weird otherwise
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = industry
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { IRE_investment_milestone = 19 }
			}
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		}
	}
}

 # MIOs #

country_event = { #A check for the H&W MIO to set research speed (donotlog)
	id = ireland.5000

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		set_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus = 3 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus = 119.building_level@dockyard }

		set_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus = 5 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus = 119.building_level@industrial_complex }
		add_to_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus = 100 }

		set_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus = 9 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus = 119.building_level@arms_factory }
		divide_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus = 2 }
		clamp_temp_variable = { var = IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus min = 0 max = 5 }

		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus = 0.01 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus = 0.01 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus = 0.01 }

		mio:IRE_harland_wolff_organisation = {
			set_mio_research_bonus = var:IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus
			set_mio_funds_gain_factor = var:IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus
			set_mio_design_team_assign_cost = var:IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus
		}

		mio:IRE_harland_wolff_expanded_organisation = {
			set_mio_research_bonus = var:IRE_harland_wolff_dockyard_bonus
			set_mio_funds_gain_factor = var:IRE_harland_wolff_civilian_bonus
			set_mio_design_team_assign_cost = var:IRE_harland_wolff_military_bonus
		}

		country_event = { id = ireland.5000 days = 7 }
	}
}

 # AI Pathing #
 ### These are based on calculations done by El Daddy, and will add up to intended values when combined. Please don't tweak without asking. ###

country_event = {  # Pathing IRE_pick_UCFpath. The flag is cleared after the UCF game.
	id = ireland.5500
	title = ireland.5500.t
	desc = ireland.5500.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1
	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes
	trigger = { is_ai = yes }

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.5500 option ireland.5500.a"
		name = ireland.5500.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_MULCAHY_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_CURSED_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ww	# Wins the BM game outright
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.5500 option ireland.5500.b"
		name = ireland.5500.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_COLLINS_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_CURSED_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_wl	# Wins the eco part
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.5500 option ireland.5500.c"
		name = ireland.5500.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_COLLINS_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_CURSED_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_lw	# Wins the northern part
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.5500 option ireland.5500.e"
		name = ireland.5500.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_COLLINS_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_election option = IRE_ELECTION_MULCAHY_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UCFpath_ll	# Loses both parts
	}
}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = IRE_PATH_SYNDIE } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_polpath_isp
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.5800 option ireland.5800.b"
		name = ireland.5800.b	# O'Donnell
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_elecpath_radical
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = IRE_PATH_TOTALIST } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = IRE_PATH_TOTALIST } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_polpath_se
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.5800 option ireland.5800.c"
		name = ireland.5800.c	# RadSocs
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_elecpath_radical }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = IRE_path option = IRE_PATH_RADSOC } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Resistance Events #

country_event = { # IRA Resistance boot event
	id = ireland.6500

	title = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = no }
		text = ireland.6500.t1
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		text = ireland.6500.t2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = no }
		text = ireland.6500.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		text = ireland.6500.d2
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_civil_war2

	trigger = {
		is_british_tag = yes
		NOT = { country_exists = IRE }
		NOT = { has_idea = IRE_IRA_UVF_resistance_idea }
		NOT = { has_idea = IRE_IRA_resistance_idea }
		is_subject = no
		IRE = {
			any_core_state = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = annexation_resistance_target scope = ROOT }
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 45
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.6500 option ireland.6500.a"
		name = ireland.6500.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			add_ideas = IRE_IRA_UVF_resistance_idea
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = IRE_IRA_resistance_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ireland.6501 days = 90 random_days = 30 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.6502 days = 180 random_days = 60 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.6503 days = 150 random_days = 50 }
			country_event = { id = ireland.6504 days = 270 random_days = 90 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Riots in Ireland
	id = ireland.6501
	title = ireland.6501.t
	desc = ireland.6501.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_civil_war2

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = IRE_IRA_resistance_idea
			has_idea = IRE_IRA_UVF_resistance_idea
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ireland.6501 option ireland.6501.a"
		name = ireland.6501.a
		add_political_power = -10
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = IRE
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = annexation_resistance_target scope = ROOT }
				resistance < 90
			}
			add_resistance = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ireland.6501 days = 90 random_days = 30 }
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

		}
	}

country_event = {  # 1916 hidden event (donotlog)
	id = irelandflavour.0
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = irelandflavour.0 days = 365 }
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_spindler_event }
			country_event = irelandflavour.2
			clr_country_flag = IRE_spindler_event
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = IRE_1916_entente_event }
			country_event = irelandflavour.3
			clr_country_flag = IRE_1916_entente_event
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes }
			country_event = irelandflavour.4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { IRE_has_natpop_govt = yes }
			country_event = irelandflavour.5
		}
		else = { country_event = irelandflavour.1 }
	}
}

country_event = {  # Canada/GBR has died
	id = irelandflavour.7			### can be triggered by on_actions
	title = irelandflavour.7.t

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_ally_with = ENT
				has_country_flag = IRE_had_war_with_ENT
			}
		}
		text = irelandflavour.7.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { is_ally_with = ENT }
		text = irelandflavour.7.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = IRE_had_war_with_ENT }
		text = irelandflavour.7.d3
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_weeping

	trigger = {
		IRE_has_puppet_govt = no
		controls_state = 119
		GBR = { exists = no }
		CAN = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = ENT
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.7 option irelandflavour.7.a"
		name = irelandflavour.7.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = no
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
			}
			add_political_power = 25
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # WCA wins ACW
	id = irelandflavour.8
	title = irelandflavour.8.t

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_parliamentary_govt = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition }
		}
		text = irelandflavour.8.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				IRE_has_pataut_govt = yes
				has_country_flag = IRE_govt_cursed_coalition
			}
		}
		text = irelandflavour.8.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_natpop_govt = yes }
		text = irelandflavour.8.d3
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes }
		text = irelandflavour.8.d4
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_WCA_militia
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_subject = no
			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_GER_victory
			has_country_flag = IRE_gateway_ENG_victory
		}
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		WCA = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
		}
		INT = { exists = yes }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.8 option irelandflavour.8.a"
		name = irelandflavour.8.a
		trigger = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = no }
		add_political_power = -5
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.025
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.8 option irelandflavour.8.b"
		name = irelandflavour.8.b
		trigger = { IRE_has_socialist_govt = yes }
		add_political_power = 25
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.025 }
		IRE_ruling_government_popularity_change = yes
	}
}
